Wuhan Garrison Command Executes Communists

Hankou Correspondence: The Wuhan Garrison Command previously received a report from the Wuchang Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Hankou Municipal Public Security Bureau that they had captured two communist leaders, Cheng Zhiqi and Meng Shangde, and two followers, Cheng Runwu and Song Mingde, and one suspect, Ren Yuzhong, and Liu Weiruo, a member of the school board, at a primary school in Hankou. Liu, etc., were indeed a misunderstanding and were immediately released on bail. Cheng, etc., were handed over to the military court for trial. The court sentenced Cheng Runwu and Song Mingde to six years of imprisonment for their following and supporting actions. Ren Yuzhong was found not guilty and released on bail. Cheng Zhiqi and Meng Shangde were convicted of counter-revolution and sentenced to death. Yesterday, on the 3rd, they were executed by beheading near the Hankou Primary School in Special District 3. In the past, communists in Hankou were executed by shooting. This is the first time that execution by beheading has been carried out. The following is the announcement of the Garrison Command: The case is based on the report of Su Shian, Director of the Wuchang Municipal Public Security Bureau, that Cheng Zhiqi and Meng Shangde, two communist leaders who were gathering crowds for riots, were captured in Yi Sanli, Hankou, and handed over to the headquarters. The military court was ordered to try them and conduct a thorough investigation. It was confirmed that Cheng Zhiqi and Meng Shangde had gathered more than a hundred party members and forcibly invaded Hanyang No. 3 Middle School, forcibly expelling the workers of the school, and continued to coerce the students of Yi Sanli Primary School in Hankou to leave the school. They also served as chairman and recorder, respectively, and resolved to launch a major riot in Yiyuan on a scheduled date, and shouted reactionary slogans. At a time when the reaction is tense and people are panicked, the criminals dared to carry out such a riot in an area full of soldiers and police, with the intention of subverting the party and the country. Their fierce flames of disregarding the government and the rules can be seen. If they are not punished to the fullest extent of the law, there will be no way to curb the revolt and suppress the chaos. Cheng Zhiqi and Meng Shangde should be sentenced to death in accordance with Articles 5 of the Martial Law and Articles 2, 1 and 2 of the Provisional Law for the Punishment of Counter-Revolutionaries, respectively, in order to serve as a warning. In addition to signing the order to bring the criminals to the execution ground to verify their identities and execute them, it is urgently announced for general knowledge. Cheng Zhiqi, 27 years old, from Qichun; Meng Shangde, 27 years old, from Zhuxi. (August 4th)

Military Progress in Fujian Province

The Six Detained by Lu are Still Safe

Fuzhou Correspondence: The military operations in Fujian Province are progressing. The 56th Division's troops on the western front have altered their original plan to advance directly along the river. Instead, they will proceed through Da Xiao Xie to Dahu, nearing the Minqing border. The northern route has crossed Beiling and Cailing, advancing towards Gutian. The southern route was originally under the command of Lin Shouguo, the 2nd Brigade Commander of the Marine Corps. However, due to Gao Weiguo and Chen Guohui vying for the defense of Quanzhou, and Gao's troops clashing with the local militia, Yang Shuzhuang specifically ordered Lin to Quanzhou to mediate. Meanwhile, Chen Guohui's troops were ordered to concentrate in Yongchun, awaiting further orders, while Gao Weiguo's troops were to retreat to Huian for their original defense, handing Quanzhou over to Lin's brigade to quell the dispute. Yesterday, Lin telegraphed the province, stating that he had transferred Chen Mingyang's regiment to Quanzhou for defense. However, the long-standing animosity between the militia and Gao's troops is on the verge of erupting, and the local order has not yet been restored after the battles, requiring suppression. Temporarily, it is feared that they will not be able to return to the province. The provincial authorities, in their military campaign against Lu's forces, have requested that the Lin Bingzhou regiment stationed in Nangang be responsible for the southern route, advancing from Yongtai. Yesterday, Liu and Huang responded to the call and entered the province to receive operational plans and replenish military supplies. Ying Zhen, the liaison officer dispatched by the headquarters to Fujian, has gone to southern Fujian to contact Zhang Zhen and Fang Shengtao to coordinate everything. Furthermore, Yan Er'ai, the Deputy Commander of the 56th Division, also returned to the province on July 26th, bringing with him 3,000 Northwestern Army prisoners of war. The division has assigned them to various regiments to participate in the operations. Fang Shengtao, the Special Military Commissioner for the southern Fujian front, has established the Special Military Commissioner's Office in Quanzhou and was inaugurated on the 26th. Currently, Zhang Zhen's division, Wang Zuqing's regiment, and Xiao Shuxuan's regiment of the provincial defense forces have assembled in Tong'an. Chen Guohui's brigade of the provincial defense forces has assembled in Yongchun, ready to advance towards Dehua and Datian. Lu Xingrong considers Dehua and Datian as the rear of Youxi. If there are any changes, it will inevitably shake the foundations, so he must vigorously resist. Therefore, on one hand, he colludes with local bandits in the two counties, including Xu Feilong, Xu Feifeng, You Cifu, and Huang Qilan, to guard the key passes. On the other hand, he deploys Jin Handing's division of rebel troops and Wei Chu's unit to serve as the first line of defense. However, it is reported that Lu's troops have switched from offense to defense. Furthermore, the two counties of Zhenghe and Songxi, previously occupied by Lu's troops in collusion with the bandit He Jinbiao, have been attacked by the provincial government, ordering Liu Zongyi of the 2nd Brigade of the Provincial Police to lead troops to advance from Shouning and Ningde. Currently, Liu has recovered the county seat of Zhenghe, and He's bandits are retreating towards Songxi. Yesterday, Liu telegraphed the province, requesting assistance with ammunition for the advance and pursuit. Since the outbreak of war near the Fujian border and the retreat of Lu's forces, conflicting reports have been circulating here regarding the fate of the five provincial commissioners and one bureau chief detained in Youxi and Yanping. Recently, British and American consuls brought missionaries from their respective countries from Yanping to the province, but they only stated that they had not heard any news of the six's deaths, which is not sufficient to be considered conclusive evidence. Upon investigation, on the 19th, Lin Zhiyuan, Chen Naiyuan, Xu Xianshi, and others sent letters from Youxi to their families, stating that the six were still in the Sanshan Guild Hall and Nanjun Guild Hall in Youxi. The letters were sent to a Mr. Chen at the Surveying Bureau for forwarding. However, Chen Naiyuan's letter stated that the weather was hot, and his old illness had recurred. The previously sent digestive and bowel cleansing medications had been used up. He hoped that the hospital director of the Boai Hospital would be consulted to prepare the medications and send them by express mail. He feared that transportation delays might prevent swift delivery. This seems to prove that the six are not dead. (July 29th)

Likouyi Iron Mine to be Exploited

The iron ore from the Likouyi Iron Mine in Tongshan County, Jiangsu Province, has been verified by chemical analysis experts to have a composition of over 65%. However, due to inconvenient transportation, its exploitation has been delayed. Recently, it was heard that Zhao Weishu, the General Manager of Lihua Iron Mining Company, has signed a long-term transportation contract with the railway authorities and is jointly investing in cooperation with the Road and Mining Department of Xinghua Bank, located at No. 48 Sichuan Road, Shanghai. On the 30th of last month, Lu Duyong, the General Manager of Xinghua Bank, signed various contracts for investment and ore sales with Zhao Weishu in the capital. Subsequently, the purchasing rights for the iron ore produced by the mine will be exclusively handled by Xinghua Bank, and mining operations have already commenced. This year, the initial output will be 100,000 tons, which will be shipped overseas in the near future to alleviate the shortage of gold and low value of silver.

First Examination for County Magistrates in Jiangsu Province

The second examination for county magistrates in Jiangsu Province was held today (the 5th) at Zhenjiang Middle School. The circumstances of the examination site are recorded below.

Entrance

Around 5:00 AM, test-takers thronged the entrance of the Provincial Middle School at Gulougang, shoulder to shoulder, approaching in the dim morning light. Ye Chucang, the Chief Examiner, had stayed overnight at the site the day before. He rose before dawn and, accompanied by the Administrative Director (Secretary-General of the Provincial Government) Jin Baoguang, inspected the premises. At 5:45 AM, the bell rang for assembly.

Roll Call

A platform was set up in the center of the assembly hall's stage. Chairman Ye, wearing a silver Chief Examiner badge and a white summer cloth gown, stood upright in the center, holding a red cinnabar pen. To his left was Zhong Shangbin, the supervising officer from the High Court, and to his right was Shen Shu'an (from the Civil Affairs Department), the roll caller. Test papers were arranged on a long table in front of the platform. Jin Baoguang, Guan Ji'an, Lu Changgui, and photo comparison staff stood on both sides. More than 300 candidates stood waiting to be called. First, the number was called, then the name. After the photo comparison staff nodded and called "Correct," the paper distributor would hand the paper to the candidate. Some took the paper and turned to leave, while others bowed before exiting. The test paper was rectangular with a red border. On the left was written "Examination Paper, Jiangsu Provincial County Magistrate Examination Committee." A rectangular floating ticket with the number was attached to the lower center, sealed where it met the paper. A white floating slip on the right corner indicated the exam number, test room number, and seat number. There were four papers: (1) Three Principles of the People, (2) Fundamentals of National Reconstruction, (3) Strategies of National Reconstruction, and (4) History of the Chinese National Revolution. By 7:00 AM, the roll call was complete. A total of 18 people were absent.

Examination Rooms

There were nine examination rooms, all located on the second floor of the U-shaped building. Room 1 was for numbers 1 to 30, Room 2 for numbers 31 to 70, Room 3 for numbers 71 to 100, Room 4 for numbers 101 to 150, Room 5 for numbers 151 to 190, Room 6 for numbers 191 to 240, Room 7 for numbers 241 to 290, Room 8 for numbers 291 to 340, and Room 9 for numbers 341 to 381. Nine Chief Examiners were assigned to set the questions, without using mimeographs, instead writing them on the blackboard themselves. Twenty-three clerks from the Provincial Government were assigned as invigilators to monitor each room.

Arrangement

A bamboo and cloth plaque reading "Jiangsu Provincial County Magistrate Examination Site Roll Call Area" was hung over the examination site's main gate. The examination rooms were simply the original classrooms with a paper strip added, indicating the room number. The administrative office was located downstairs in the Qianjin Building. The Chief Examiners' and court supervising officer's rest rooms were upstairs. Armed guards were stationed by the Public Security Bureau from Qianqiu Bridge to the school gate. Inside the gate, in addition to the Provincial Government guard, there were more than ten members of the Provincial Public Security Team on duty. Each officer's badge or symbol was of one of five types: (1) Chief Examiner, silver badge; (2) Supervising Officer, yellow silk symbol; (3) Invigilator, red silk symbol; (4) Staff, white silk symbol; (5) Duty, blue cloth symbol. Guards were not allowed to admit anyone without the appropriate symbol.

Time

The examination time was from 7:00 AM to 11:00 AM, and could not exceed 12:00 PM. Only one female candidate was present. Among the male candidates, young men accounted for two-fifths, middle-aged men for three-fifths, and older men were two or three out of a hundred. Few wore Western suits. Two or three had white hair and appeared rather disheveled.

Exam Questions

(Strategies of National Reconstruction) (1) What is meant by psychological reconstruction? How is the theory of "knowing is difficult, acting is easy" the driving force behind pragmatism? (2) Describe the position, function, and purpose of the three major ports: northern, eastern, and southern. (3) Why did the Premier attach great importance to the book "Fundamentals of Civil Rights"? (Fundamentals of National Reconstruction) (1) Why did the Premier establish a tutelage period between the military and constitutional periods? Please explain. (2) What is the difference between tutelage and one-party rule? Briefly discuss the current party rule in Russia and Italy. (3) The county is the unit of self-government. Based on the Fundamentals of National Reconstruction, draft a plan for county self-government. (History of the Chinese Revolution) (1) Our party has changed its name five times, from the Revive China Society to the Kuomintang. Briefly describe the process of each name change. (2) Describe the reasons for, the significance of, and the impact on the National Revolution of the party's reorganization in 1924. (3) When were the Second and Third National Congresses of the party held? How did the National Revolution progress between these two congresses? (4) Describe the general situation of the National Revolution after the Third National Congress. (Three Principles of the People) (1) County party headquarters and county governments often experience conflicts and disputes. How should the county magistrate cooperate with the county party headquarters to ensure the smooth progress of county party affairs, politics, and local self-government? (2) Suppose communists and statists infiltrate the county, enticing young people to attempt reactionary activities. As a county magistrate, from the party's perspective, draft a letter advising all the youth in the county. (3) Recently, so-called proletarian literature has advocated communist fallacies, provoking class struggle. How should we promote Three Principles of the People art and literature to stop it?

Local Correspondence

Fengxian

District Office Investigates Suspected Kidnapping Case

The county government previously reported a case based on information from Chen Jinfa, the chief of the Eighth Precinct, that Fang Bokang, the ringleader in the kidnapping of a Lu family member in Zhuangxing, had identified He Guichan, also known as Yao Jun, as an accomplice. The precinct dispatched a secret agent to apprehend him, but he was unexpectedly intercepted and released by Yang Xingsheng, the chief of the Second Platoon of police stationed in Zhuangxing, in front of the platoon headquarters. Despite repeated negotiations, Yang has only promised to return him, with ongoing prevarications. County Magistrate Shen deemed the case significant and found it necessary to investigate He Guixiang's potential involvement. Consequently, he instructed Zhang Fengtai, the chief of the Eighth District, to conduct an impartial investigation. The report states that after the Lu family kidnapping occurred in the Pandian Township of the district, the family received a letter from the kidnappers demanding a ransom. Lu Ziyun, the clan elder, entrusted He Guixiang, a local who currently serves as a captain of a smuggling suppression vessel, to negotiate in Shanghai. However, the negotiation failed due to a disagreement over the price, and the police also ordered him to purchase informants, but to no avail. Ultimately, the capture of the notorious bandits on July 8th was due to a confidential report from the Shanghai Security Corps, assisted by Yang, the platoon leader. While He Guixiang's involvement in the case cannot be fully clarified, the Lu family did entrust him to contact the kidnapper Liu Boxian, also known as Fang Bokang, once. It is possible that the kidnappers mistakenly believed him to be the informant, leading to resentment and complications. However, the Lu family has repeatedly stated that He had no connection to the case after that one contact and is willing to vouch for him. Therefore, the precinct's claim that he is a wanted criminal is unfounded. The allegation that Platoon Leader Yang intercepted and released him is even more speculative. Since He Guixiang was not involved in the case, the platoon leader had no reason to detain him at the platoon headquarters. There was no interception, let alone release. If the Eighth Precinct believes he is connected to the case, they should have dispatched police to escort him. However, according to the platoon headquarters, only one agent arrived at the time and did not explicitly state anything. As everyone saw it, it does not seem to be a false claim. Therefore, the platoon leader could not have known. In conclusion, the main culprits in the Lu family kidnapping have been apprehended, and the truth is known to all. No innocent people should be implicated, lest those who handle the case become discouraged. It is now understood that County Magistrate Shen has reviewed the district's report and, except for dismissing the allegations against Platoon Leader Yang, has ordered He Guixiang to voluntarily surrender himself for questioning, as his involvement falls within the scope of the judiciary.

Qingpu

Misunderstanding Involving Police Officer and Local Militia

On the afternoon of August 1st, two patrol boats from the Fifth Water Police Team were sailing from Songjiang back to Jiading, passing through Chonggu Town in the county. They moored in the South Market for the night. Five or six plainclothes patrol officers, including Lu Akun, went ashore for leisure. Li Xueyu, a militiaman from the town's security corps, encountered them while on patrol and, considering their behavior suspicious, questioned them. The police officers refused to explain and resorted to violence, beating Li, who was outnumbered, until he was injured and fled back to the corps headquarters. When Zhou, the corps commander, learned of this, he dispatched the entire corps, armed with live ammunition, to apprehend the officers. The townspeople mistakenly believed that bandits had arrived, causing great chaos. Just as panic was spreading, Officers Wang and Hu learned of the situation and went to the corps headquarters to mediate. Only then did the truth come to light. However, militiaman Li Xueyu's injuries were quite severe, so he was hired a boat that night and sent to the city hospital for treatment. The corps also submitted a report to the county government, requesting a decision.

Business Competition Leads to Dispute

Yichangfu Clothing Store in Chonggu Town has been in business for over a decade. Recently, to expand its business, it began selling silk and foreign cloth, leading to intense business competition with Guangfengyi Silk and Foreign Goods Store across the street. A few days ago, a Mr. Dai purchased a Zhang of gauze from Guangfengyi but returned it because he did not like the pattern. Guangfengyi immediately accused Yichangfu Clothing Store of instigating the return, leading to a dispute. The town's chamber of commerce dispatched members to mediate and hold a meeting. The result was that Guangfengyi had no evidence and should not have falsely accused Yichangfu, and formally apologized to Yichangfu Clothing Store.

Prelude to Construction of New Prison

The Jiangsu High Court, in order to improve the prisons in each county, dispatched Shi Zeren to Qingpu for inspection. As a result, it was determined that the prison could be improved to a certain extent, but the detention center needed to be completely rebuilt. The court consulted with the county government and local agencies to discuss solutions. They decided to first organize design and fundraising teams to carry out everything. All district chiefs in the county are ex officio members of the prison construction committee, and Zhu Hua, Shen Yansheng, and Yang Lucun were appointed as members of the charter drafting committee. It is said that the construction cost is about 4,000 yuan.

Solution to Changing Qingpu-Shanghai Route

The long-distance bus route from Qingpu to the airfield was started in the spring and could have been completed long ago. However, the airfield authorities intervened, stating that the land was within a military area and subject to frequent curfews, so the route had to be changed. After submitting a request to the provincial authorities, negotiations with the Ministry of Military Affairs were unsuccessful. The route has now been changed and the measurement has been completed. It only crosses into Shanghai City, but it is reported that the construction bureau chief has made an informal contact with the Shanghai Municipal Public Works Bureau, so there should be no problems.

Songjiang

Haining Traveler's Suicide Attempt Foiled

The defenses of this city have recently been tightened. Zhu Huanbo, the chief of the Public Security Bureau, personally patrols late at night, paying particular attention to out-of-town travelers to prevent bandits from sneaking in. Yesterday (the 4th) around 11:00 PM, Chief Zhu was patrolling Liaodong Hotel and found Zhu Mianzhen in Room 3 acting suspiciously. There were two bottles of sleeping pills, "Medina," on the bedside table, further arousing his suspicions, as well as a letter to his sister. He learned that Zhu had only taken one pill and was not in serious danger. He was taken to the bureau for interrogation. Zhu confessed that he was 21 years old and from Haining. He had been working in a silk factory in Shanghai but had lost his job and was destitute, so he decided to commit suicide. He has a mother and sister at home, etc. The gist of his suicide letter was that he was unlucky, had suffered many setbacks, and voluntarily took poison to commit suicide. His letter to his sister, signed Meizhen, said that she was a virtuous sister and he could not handle the entrusted matters, so please handle it yourself. He could not repay her kindness in this life and would repay her in the next. However, the wording was unclear, so it seems that he was from the working class and was suffering from economic oppression. Chief Zhu, out of concern for human life, ordered him to be detained at the bureau and requested the Haining Public Security Bureau to notify his family to pick him up to prevent him from taking his own life again.

Auction of Clothing and Jewelry Looted from Sijing Pawnshops

Regarding the case of the looting of Sijing Town by lake bandits, it is now known that the clothing and jewelry looted from Qingyuxiang and He two pawnshops were previously sealed by the county committee, etc. Having been approved for auction, they were transported to Songjiang yesterday and auctioned at the Pawn Industry Association under the supervision of the County Chamber of Commerce, the Sijing District Office of the Chamber of Commerce, and members of the County Government. The jewelry was won by Rifeng and Defeng Silver Shops, and the cloth clothing was won by Xiangtai.

Suzhou

Detailed Account of Water Police Repelling Lake Bandits

Lin Guoliang, the temporary commander of the Taihu bandit suppression, opened fire on bandits at Nanku Xinkai Road, across from Hengjing Maoqi Port, at 11:00 AM on the 4th. The fierce battle lasted until around 5:00 PM, when it subsided. At that time, Wang Wusheng, the captain of the 8th Team of the Water Police, patrol officer Huang Renmin, and one hostage were rescued. The details of this have already been reported in yesterday's special telegram section. The details at the time will be recorded again as follows: At about 9:00 AM on the 4th, Commander Gong received a report that more than 300 lake bandits were gathering on more than 30 boats in the Nanku Xinkai Road area, planning to flee to Zhejiang Province. After receiving the report, Gong immediately ordered the distribution of each team to pre-deploy defense lines and design encirclement and suppression. The 6th and 10th teams of the Second District Water Police blocked Tingzi Port, the 7th team was stationed in Hengjing, the 8th team guarded Dongshan, the 15th team of the Third District and the guerrilla team were stationed in Caogang, the 12th team guarded the Yangcheng Lake pass, and the 13th team was stationed at the Changshu Guanpu estuary to block pirates from entering the country. Commander Gong himself led the 11th and 14th teams to advance on the central road. Once all arrangements were in place, he ordered the 14th Team Leader Huai Zongbang, the 15th Team Leader Lu Shangzhong, and the guerrilla team leader Fang to carry out a three-way encirclement. At about 11:00 AM, the bandits were already surrounded. Gong led the 11th Team from the central road to the destination and ordered them to fire on the bandits. The bandit leaders ordered the members to fight back, and the fierce battle lasted for six hours. At about 5:30 PM, the bandits were overwhelmed and fled. In this battle, two bandit ships were shot down and the hostage, the son of Wang Wusheng, the captain of the 8th Team, patrol officer Huang Wangmin, and Chen Huimin, the head of the Dongshan Security Corps, were rescued. Three bandits were captured and one banner of the bandit was shot down, with the words "Jiangsu-Zhejiang Taihu Guerrilla Team of the Navy, Army, and Air Force" written on it, and a large character "Woman" in the center. A number of firearms and more than ten bandits were killed or wounded. After the lake bandits fled, one road fled to Yichangxing and one road fled to Yanmu. Seeing that the bandits had escaped, Commander Gong rescued the hostages and arrived at Hengjing that night to contact local people and convened the 11th Team Leader Xu Boying, the 14th Team Leader Huai Zongbang, the 15th Team Leader Lu Shangzhong, the 7th Team Leader Li Jianxun, and the guerrilla team leader Fang to plan the second step of the encirclement and suppression. He still ordered each team to block the key passes and telegraphed the district office. Moreover, the gentry of Dongshan and Hengjing met with Commander Gong yesterday morning, stating that Captain Wang Wusheng was already out of danger, but there were still 27 hostages who had not been rescued. They requested that Commander Gong actively rescue the other hostages. In addition to comforting them, Commander Gong also promised to do his best to find a solution.

Re-examination of Death-Uncertain Lawsuit Scheduled

The case of the death of Han Jinshi, the daughter-in-law of Han Gunong in Gejialong, Guomen Nei, was reported in February of this year by her relatives Han Guoduo and Han Guolin, who claimed that Han Jinshi's death was planned by the treacherous servant Shi Junqing and Chen Lishi. The prosecutor's office of the District Court exhumed the body and examined the bones. As Han Jinshi had no evidence of wrongdoing, Han Guoduo and Han Guolin were sentenced to imprisonment for the crime of attempting to extort money, and Shi Junqing and Chen Lishi were released without charge. Han Guoduo and his brothers expressed dissatisfaction and appealed to the High Court. The High Court approved the appeal and scheduled a hearing for 9:00 AM on the 20th of this month.

Wujiang

Gang of Bandits Robs Six Families in Beidagang

At 12:00 AM on the 3rd, a gang of more than 20 bandits speaking with Jiangbei accents and carrying firearms suddenly broke into the homes of six farmers, including Jiang Yongchun, in Beidagang Village, nine Li outside the east gate of this city. They looted everything from the chests and cabinets, fired several shots before leaving, and calmly boarded a boat and fled.

Wuxi

Accelerated Construction of Huanhu Avenue

The Jiang-Zhejiang Provincial Governments initiated the construction of the Huanhu Avenue. The Construction Department sent personnel to Wuxi to survey and decided to build the Huanhu Avenue from Xucang in this county along the shore of Taihu Lake directly to Yixing. Recently, Construction Department Director Sun sent the highway bureau survey team leader Sun Baoqin, a local, with more than ten team members by car to Wuxi from the province yesterday afternoon to remeasure the route in order to promote the realization of the road.

Suspect Arrested in Gun Loss Case

At the township of Shiqiwan, District 16 of the county, a rice sale was held on the 4th, and buyers were very crowded. The local merchant corps sent members to maintain order. A member of the corps placed a Mauser pistol in his pocket and hung it on the wall during lunchtime. When he went to retrieve it after the meal, the gun and clothing were gone. He immediately searched around and arrested Tang, a suspect, in Qianzhou township, District 15, and recovered five bullets, which were indeed bullets for the gun. However, the gun has not been recovered and is still being investigated.

Chen Lunkuai Transferred to County for Interrogation

Chen Lunkuai, a resident of Anzhen, Huaixia Township, District 8, was re-arrested and transferred to the bureau for interrogation. Xie Weikang, a communist suspect, was also arrested. It is heard that Xie is a native of Zhenjiang who lives in Anzhen and runs a teahouse, and Chen Lunkuai often visits him. The reason for Chen's re-arrest is that Chen was wanted for communist activities in this county. When Chen was arrested and sent to the court in Rugao, the High Court found that Chen had not committed a crime in Rugao, but did not revoke the local files for verification, so he was acquitted and released. Recently, Chen returned to Wuxi and was secretly ordered by County Magistrate Sun to have Chen arrested and investigated by the Anzhen Public Security 16th Branch Bureau. Yesterday, Public Security Bureau Chief Xu presented Chen and Xie to the county government. Tang Yiqin, a member of the backlog clearance committee, opened a court hearing. Chen Lunkuai's confession was vague. Xie Weikang confessed that he had not joined the Communist Party. At the end of the interrogation, Chen Lunkuai was ordered to be transferred to the Jiangsu High Court for interrogation, and Xie Weikang was temporarily detained for investigation and verification.

Changzhou

County Reorganization Council's Anti-Theft Meeting

The Wuyi County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee held its first meeting on the afternoon of the 4th to discuss anti-theft measures because the rampant banditry and robbery in the villages were causing daily injuries and deaths. (1) Organize a guerrilla team composed of the police team and the merchant corps, and request the local garrison to participate to carry out the suppression in the four villages. (2) The county magistrate should issue a notice to all district chiefs that anyone who discovers suspicious people must report them to the authorities immediately, otherwise, the district chief will be severely punished if a theft occurs in the district. (3) Please notify the county government to reward people for reporting information about bandits. The authorities should keep the informants strictly confidential and set reward methods. (4) The County Court should issue a notice that the punishment of bandits will not be based on codified law, but on the newly promulgated regulations on the punishment of bandits.

Provincial Inspector Investigates Accusation

The Education Department has appointed Inspector Cao Shutian to Changzhou to investigate the case against Yu Zigang, the principal of Wuyi County Middle School. After Cao came to Changzhou, he investigated each point of the accusation. The department paid particular attention to the economic part and obtained the account books from the school for verification. He will return to the department on the 6th to report.

Jiading

New Prison Completed

A few days ago, County Magistrate Chen initiated the construction of a new prison with 31 rooms because the county prison was narrow and insufficient. In addition to submitting a report to the provincial authorities for record, he invited the local gentry to solicit donations separately. The Zhang Hengxing carpentry shop contracted the project for more than 7,000 yuan. Construction began on May 1 and has now been fully completed. The province has sent the Shanghai county magistrate to Jiading today to inspect and accept the prison.

Smuggling Offender Arrested

Yao Alian, who lives in the North Market of Xuhang town outside the east gate, is a rascal who has been wandering outside for many years. He recently returned to Xuhang to sell opium. He was caught by the Xuhang branch office yesterday and the day before. Twelve liang of opium and three cans of opium ash were seized on the spot and sent to the County Public Security Bureau for judicial action.

Zhenjiang

Jiangsu Provincial Government Pays Attention to Local Security

The Jiangsu Provincial Government's bandit suppression measures have recently shown signs of progress, and the organization of an eight-county joint defense has also been planned. As for the bandit problems in the Huaihai area, the provincial government has planned for the bandit suppression methods in detail because the area is remote and beyond reach. The source of the bandits in the area is probably due to the people's difficult living conditions, and the coastal fishing industry has recently failed, resulting in more and more fishermen becoming thieves. In view of this, the provincial government is planning for fishermen relief methods and formulating various fishing industry protection regulations to prevent the failure of the fishing industry, fundamentally prevent fishermen from becoming pirates, and avoid increasing the strength of other bandits. On the one hand, the Security Department will concentrate its forces to do its best to suppress the bandits. Regarding the communist bandit problem in Jiangnan, the provincial government has ordered that they be jointly and severely suppressed for the sake of stabilizing the defense in response to the Xiang-Gui bandit riots and the lurking rebellion in various places.

Disputes over Public Property in Four Counties

The test site of Liyang County, which is public property of four counties including Jintan, Danyang, and Zhenjiang, was previously seized by local ruffian Wang Zhenchen. Representatives from the four counties held a meeting to investigate and requested the Department of Civil Affairs to allocate all the property as a fund for education and relief institutions. This was already approved by the provincial government meeting. Yesterday, another meeting was held at the county party headquarters to discuss countermeasures. The representatives resolved the following measures: (1) State the reasons why the public property belongs to the four counties, and submit them separately to the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government, requesting reconsideration and revocation of the original proposal to establish public undertakings for the four counties. The petition will be drafted by the representative of Danyang County. (2) Each county will send one representative to the Provincial Government and the Provincial Party Headquarters to make representations.

Yangzhou

The Department of Education's Attitude Towards the County's Education Budget

Most of the teachers and staff in the urban area of this county believe that the budget for the 19th year compiled by the county's Bureau of Education is not satisfactory, so there was a collective resignation some days ago. However, after receiving the budget, the department believed that it exceeded the standard too much and was inconvenient to accommodate. Yesterday, a section of the department sent a letter to Director Chen, inviting him to go to the province for a face-to-face discussion. It is said that Director Chen plans to cross the river early tomorrow (the 5th).

Inspection Office Arrests Suspicious Passengers

Yesterday (the 3rd) at 3:00 AM, the patrol team of the joint military and police inspection office of this city arrested a guest named Jiang in Room 7 of the Luyang Inn on Xinsheng Street. Jiang claimed to be a staff member of the Confidential Office of the Xu, Huai, and Hai Guerrilla Headquarters. The team asked him what his mission was in Yangzhou. He said that he was going to Xiannv Town to guard the funds of You, and to handle the slaughter tax of this county. He also claimed to know Shao Yaoqing, who is currently a slaughter tax official. Shao lives in Beixiaojie in this city. The team then went to arrest Shao and took him to the office together. Less than two hours later, another Jiang, who also claimed to be an adjutant of the Guerrilla Headquarters, came. He had gone out for business, and when he returned, he learned that the former had been arrested. He took a car to the inspection office to inquire and was also detained. The inspection office has now telegraphed the Guerrilla Headquarters to inquire about the truth, and a decision will be made after receiving a reply.

The Nantong Party and government organs planned to establish a temporary rehabilitation center to handle the surrender of communists and submitted it to the province for approval. They have now been ordered that a reflection院(court affiliated to the High Court to reform communist ideology) will be established soon, and the request should not be discussed.

Headquarters Orders Recovered Soldiers to Return to Their Units

The General Headquarters telegraphed the Chong County Government and the 31st Rear Hospital for Wounded Soldiers to report the roster of recovered soldiers. County Magistrate Zhang and Director Cao immediately complied. The General Headquarters specially sent a commissioner to Nantong to handle the return of the soldiers to their units.

Jiangyin

Frequent Bandit Cases, Plan to Add Police Squad

The county government meeting was held yesterday and decided on important cases. Due to the frequent bandit cases in the county and the weakness of the current forces, it is proposed to add a temporary police squad to strengthen defense. It was decided that the police squad should be established immediately in view of the actual needs. However, the annual cost of the squad is about 7,500 yuan, which cannot be raised for the time being. It is proposed to request the province to allow the temporary borrowing from the agricultural mu tax for improvement, and then raise funds to compensate. As for the firearms, the Finance Bureau was ordered to raise an additional 1,000 yuan in accordance with the previous county government resolution for the purchase.

Using Labor Unrest to Commit Crimes, Sent to High Court

The workers Ren Ruisheng and Li Junsan, who were involved in the case of using the May 30th yarn factory labor unrest to commit crimes, were interrogated repeatedly. Because of their involvement in reactionary relations, they were escorted to the Suzhou High Court on the 5th by police officer Chen for interrogation.

Half a Day of Disturbances, Fortunately Calmed Down

On the morning of the 4th, eight or nine gangsters speaking Hakka dialect were arguing with the guards at the county government site. They then went to the Taidong and Jiaotong hotels outside the north gate to cause trouble. The joint military and police inspection team went to stop them, but a box cannon and bullets were snatched, and the squad leader was injured in the head with a bowl. Several of the rioters fired the snatched box cannon along the road from Zhongshan Gate, causing chaos in the Dongda Street area. A large team of military and police rushed to the scene, and the rioters took rickshaws to the south gate. Another large team of military and police surrounded the south gate and recovered the stolen gun, capturing four rioters. The detective team captured four people on Xida Street, and County Magistrate Li captured four people in Nan Suo Lane and other places. All were taken to the Gendarmerie Company Inspection Office. Local agencies and Commander Yang of the fortress telegraphed their superiors to handle the matter. During the disturbance, Dongda Street and the front of the county government were under special guard, and traffic was cut off. The situation was tense until about 6:00 PM, when the guards were lifted.

Jiashan

Rumors of Robbery in Yu Hui Town

It is said that in Yu Hui Town, which belongs to this county, more than 30 bandit ships sailed in from the eastern countryside at noon yesterday (the 3rd). Some refugees and vagrants mixed in and robbed by force, extorting 1,800 yuan. The local people could not cope and only raised 400 yuan. The bandits were dissatisfied and threatened to rob the whole town. According to reports from the escapees, the 8th Squadron of the water police has gone to intercept and suppress the bandits, who have already sailed southwest. The 7th Squadron has sent a team to assist in the suppression. Xitang and Fengjing, which are nearby, have been properly guarded.

Arrested Bandits Escorted to the County for Interrogation

The Yao Zhuang Bridge Town Security Corps of Shan County arrested two bandits, Zhang Er and Shen Lanchun, during a midnight patrol some days ago. They were immediately escorted to the county government, where they were interrogated by County Magistrate Liang before being transferred to the court for investigation.

Ting Wu Accusation Case Transferred to Hangzhou for Trial

The case in which former County Public Security Bureau Chief Gu Xiaokuan and former Fengjing Branch Chief Wu Jinming accused each other in the county court was ordered by the Hangzhou District Court to submit all case documents for a joint trial. Therefore, the county court issued a notice to suspend the trial.

Ningbo

Robbery Case in Yanjiacun

Yesterday morning, four bandits scaled the wall of Yan Shaoji's house in Yanjiacun, Maiqiao, in the western countryside of Yin County. Lin Agen, the housekeeper of the Yan family, noticed them and escaped through the back door to sound the alarm. The villagers took up farm tools and searched everywhere. At this time, the sky was already dawning, and the bandits fled in panic. Agen chased after one bandit and hit the bandit's foot with a hoe, causing the bandit to fall into the river. The bandit then took out a wooden-cased gun from the water and shot Agen dead. After killing Agen, the bandit saw the villagers standing on both banks and knew that it was difficult to escape. He also drowned. The bandit was about 24 or 25 years old, wearing a black jacket and trousers, with a wooden gun hanging in front of his chest, a knife, and a small knife. There were 12 yuan in silver dollars and some cents in the pocket of the jacket. There were no wounds on the body. The public security branch reported the case to the court for inspection. The remaining bandits all escaped.

Since Mayor Yang took office in Ningbo, the position of Director of Finance has changed hands three times in a few months. This is due to the financial difficulties and the difficulty in handling affairs. Shangyu

A Sudden Search for Firearms

Some days ago, eight or nine people who looked like soldiers and carried long guns suddenly came to the home of Lian Yanchen in Shanghutou, Songxia. Led by a person wearing a gray military uniform, they searched all the rooms upstairs and downstairs. Then, when they heard the sound of gongs in the village, the leader ordered his accomplices to raise their guns and ammunition and spread out in various places to defend themselves. Then, they forced Cao Mengshan, a resident of Zhanghu Bridge, to act as a guide and took the whole team to the Yangshan boat they had parked in advance before releasing Cao. Afterwards, the villagers speculated that Lian Yanchen had always been law-abiding, so where did the firearms come from? Some said that Lian's sister, Qian Chen (the owner of Ma Zhu Cai Zhang), had once come to her uncle's house. The person in military uniform was actually a disguised kidnapper who hoped to use this as an excuse to kidnap Chen for ransom.

At about 9:00 PM the night before last, more than ten robbers broke into the home of the late Zhang Xiaxu in Zhang Lu Village, Songxia, by breaking through a wall. They climbed upstairs and robbed the family, losing a total of two or three hundred yuan. Zhang had two sons, who had all taken their families elsewhere for business. Only the old, weak, women, and children were left in the house.

Qin Mian served as the chairman and Pan Zhijiu as the recorder. The ceremony was as follows: (A) The chairman reported: 1. Each county should have two representatives for this meeting. 2. The meeting time is from 3:00 PM on August 2nd and continues from 8:00 AM on August 3rd. (B) The Proposal Review Committee reported: 1. 38 proposals were submitted by various counties. 2. Review criteria: (1) Important proposals are submitted. (2) Proposals with the same meaning are merged. (3) Proposals that can be postponed are retained. (4) Problematic proposals are not submitted. 3. It was decided to submit 11 proposals, retain 6 proposals, and not submit 21 proposals. (C) Matters for discussion: 1. Request the Department of Education and the Ministry of Education to promote the Provincial Education Association (submitted by Jiangning, Qidong, Yizheng, and Wuxi). (Resolution) Passed. The submission will be handled by the secretariat. 2. Request the Department of Education to issue an order to all counties to establish County Education Associations within a limited time if they have not been established (submitted by Wuxi). Liyang seconded. (Resolution) Passed. The submission will be handled by the secretariat. 3. The newly promulgated budget standard for primary school expenses is not suitable for local conditions. The conference should submit a request to the Department of Education to revise it (submitted by Liuhe, Chongming, Donghai, and Kunshan). (Resolution) Passed. The attachment will be issued in the name of the conference. The declaration and submission will be handled by the secretariat. 4. Request the Department of Education to issue an order to all counties' Bureau of Education to find ways to improve teachers' salaries (submitted by Wuxi, Chongming, and Kunshan). (Resolution) Passed. The submission will be handled by the secretariat. 5. Request the Department of Education to clear up the old property of the Provincial Education Association (submitted by Wuxi). Jiangning seconded. (Resolution) Passed. The submission will be handled by the secretariat. 6. Request the Department of Education to issue an order to all provincial primary and secondary schools to give preferential treatment to teachers' children by allowing them to enter school free of charge or at least exempting them from tuition fees (submitted by Wuxi). Jiangning and Wujin seconded. (Resolution) Approved in principle, modified to be provincial and county primary and secondary schools for all levels of schools in the province, and preferential treatment for children of educators as preferential treatment for children of educational personnel. The submission will be handled by the secretariat. 7. Request the conference to resolve to issue a circular to all county Bureau of Education to allocate a certain amount of money from the annual budget (appropriately propose a percentage of the total county budget) to each County Education Association for holding branch research conferences and purchasing educational reference books (submitted by Liuhe). (Resolution) Passed and revised to be "allocate a certain amount of money from the annual budget, appropriately propose a few percent of the total county budget" to be "appropriately propose a few percent from the annual budget" to be handed over to each County Education Association. The official letter will be handled by the secretariat. 8. County Education Associations exchange publications to serve as references and communicate with each other (submitted by Wuxi). (Resolution) Passed. 9. County Education Associations should assist the Bureau of Education to effectively promote phonetic symbols (submitted by Wuxi and Chongming). (Resolution) Passed. 11. Send a letter to the Bureau of Education in each county that has not established a rural normal school to consider the local situation and establish or jointly organize it as soon as possible (Resolution) The official letter will be handled by the secretariat. 12. How should the resolutions of this conference be implemented in reality? (Resolution) In addition to submitting to the Provincial Education Association in the name of the conference, each County Education Association will submit to the Department of Education separately. 13. How should this conference handle the registration procedures? (Resolution) Passed to the Executive Committee for handling. 14. A declaration drafted by the secretariat (Resolution) Passed.

Director of the Fourth Hall, Xu Deyang, Resigns

Starting this year, the tea garden departments attached to each hall will be abolished, and guidance will be given to nearby large tea houses. (3) A proposal to revise the hall affairs form was revised and passed. (4) A proposal to establish an implementation office was resolved. Each director will contact the municipal commissioners in each district for handling. If necessary, the bureau may consult the Bureau of Health to send personnel to assist.

Compiled by Four-Corner Indexing Method

Graduation of the Second Class of the Index Practice Institute

The Commercial Press strongly advocates student vacation services. This year, it specially used the summer vacation to open the Four-Corner Indexing Method Index Practice Institute. The details of the first and second classes have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Yesterday (5th), the second class held a graduation ceremony. The attendees were Li Bake, Manager of the Press, Xiao Fang, Chief of the Confidential Section, Zhuang Baiyu, Yang Ji, Director of the Institute, He Bocheng, Li Bojia, Publishing Minister, Xu Baode, Lin Baohui, Chen Zixin, Cao Yikong, Mao Songgan, Zhao Jingyuan, Zong Youze, Cai Lufu and more than 200 interns. The chairman was Li Bake, the master of ceremonies was Zhao Jingyuan, and the recorder was Zong Youze. The ceremony was as follows: First, the chairman, Li Bake, delivered the opening speech and presented awards. Then, Director He Bocheng reported the interns' performance. Zhuang Baiyu gave a speech, and Li Bojia gave a farewell speech on behalf of the instructors. After refreshments, the meeting adjourned. The first class of the institute had 205 interns representing 103 schools, and the second class had 172 interns representing 104 schools. The two classes had a total of 377 interns representing 209 schools. According to the location of the interns' schools, there were a total of 14 provinces. It is said that the interns' indexing performance this time was excellent, and the speed of the four-corner indexing also broke the highest record of the previous sessions. In 1928, the fastest time to index a character was 2 seconds. This year, the fastest time for the first class was 10.4 seconds, and the fastest time for the second class was 8.9 seconds on average. From this, it can be seen that the four-corner indexing is indeed the most convenient method of the new indexing method. In addition, the first place in the second class was Zhao Xuan from Shanghai Middle School in this city, the second place was Chi Yunwei from Suzhou First Normal School, and the third place was He Xiaoyi from the French National Technical College in this city.

Shanghai Private Middle School, located in Pan Garden on Jiaozhou Road and Binlang Road in West Shanghai, has been operating for many years. Eating Bread Provides Strength

Bai Leshou, fighting on an empty stomach, won the first set. Lu Weiwei was unwilling to concede and fought hard for 14 games, also winning a set. At this time, Bai was extremely hungry and unable to continue. He put down his racket, bought a bread roll and a bowl of mung bean soup, and returned to the court with renewed strength, winning the decisive set 6-1.

Distracted by Work, Unable to Fight Hard

Chen Yifu's style is steady, while Wang Shouqi's is aggressive. Although their styles are different, their effectiveness is the same. The match started a little late yesterday morning, and Wang was anxious to get to work and had no intention of fighting for long. He only attacked fiercely. Chen waited for changes to the game. In the end, Wang lost 6-4, 6-2.

Using High Pressure Tactics Successfully

Wu Zangqing's shots tend to be upwards, while Zhu Xilin's tend to be downwards. Their styles are different, but both are biased. However, in the match, the one who pressed downwards had a great advantage. Although the one who received and defended ran and resisted stubbornly, he was defeated 6-4, 7-5.

The Hong Kong Chinese Nanyang Football Team Will Depart

Departure Early This Month / Return to Hong Kong in Mid-September

First to Saigon, Annam / Then to the Nanyang Islands

A Group of Twenty-Two / Led by Mr. Ye Jiugao

(July 31st, Hong Kong Dispatch) The Chinese Sports Association Football Team is famous and admired, and the people of the country have bestowed upon it the nickname "Tiger Team" because of its unassailable prowess. Since the end of the official football tournament in the spring, recognizing the long-standing admiration of the overseas Chinese in Nanyang for the team, it is planning to take this opportunity to send a team to tour Nanyang, to meet with the overseas Chinese on the green football fields, and to promote the development of sports. This is the reason for their intention. Since the South China Football Team accepted the invitation of the Singapore Chinese Sports Association to send a team to the south a month ago, Chinese football had originally wanted to follow suit, not allowing South China to be solely beautiful at the forefront. After the news spread, people in Hong Kong paid great attention to it, because South China going first and Chinese football following suit was not only an unprecedented feat, but also admired the good fortune of the people there. However, the team was unable to proceed due to various reasons at the time, and it was inconvenient to announce whether or not it would happen, so as not to allow the outside world to speculate. The reporter has repeatedly reported on the news of the team's southern tour based on dispatches from Singapore, but there have been doubts, and there have even been rumors that it will not happen. This is because Chinese football had not made a definite statement on this matter at the time, which caused people to have doubts. However, in recent days, the news of the team's revival for the southern expedition has been very clamorous. The reporter, considering the importance of the matter and the eagerness of all parties to understand, specifically inquired with the person in charge of the association, who said that this matter has been a long-cherished wish, and that it was not convenient to announce it earlier because the preparations for various matters were not yet ready. Now, after the committee has further discussed this matter, it has been decided to send a team to tour the south, and the first leg has been set for August 12th. If so, the opportunity for the team to meet with the overseas Chinese in Nanyang is not far away.

Meaning of the Name

The Chinese Sports Association originally planned to only send a team to Singapore, so the name originally planned was also only the Singapore Football Team. Now, the committee members believe that the purpose of sending a team to tour the south this time is to seek the study of football skills, so that in the next ordinary trophy football competition, they can win the championship for the fourth time and create a new record. (Chinese football has won the ordinary trophy for three consecutive times, which is already a new record.) It has been found that there are many football masters hidden in the southern islands, not just limited to Singapore, so taking advantage of this southern tour, they will also travel to other ports. Therefore, the name had to be changed. Last night, it was decided to change it to the Chinese Sports Nanyang Football Team.

Southern Tour Itinerary

It is estimated that in addition to agreeing on the name, the committee also decided on other matters regarding the sending of a team to tour the south last night. It was also decided that the southern tour team will depart on the 12th of next month on the French ship D'Artagnan. The route is to first go to Saigon and other ports in Annam, where there may be several matches, and then travel south to the Nanyang area, such as Singapore, Sandakan, Surabaya, and Java. The scheduled period is one month, and they can return to Hong Kong around mid-September to participate in the 1930-1931 ordinary football tournament in Hong Kong.

Active Practice

As for the list of players for the southern tour football team, it has not been announced yet, because some players may not be able to go due to circumstances. The team will consist of about 22 people in total. According to the reporter's investigation last night, the person in charge of the association's football department will send the strongest team to ensure a good performance during the competition. Now that the team is ready to go, they are actively training. It is also said that the leader of the team has been elected by the players, and they all have their eye on Mr. Ye Jiugao. It is found that this year, the Hong Kong teams touring the south will first have the South China Football Team, followed by the Chinese Football Team. In between, there is also the Chinese Expeditionary Team organized by the Shanghai Lehua Sports Association (players from both the South China and Chinese football teams have been selected to participate in the expedition). The overseas Chinese in Nanyang who admire the national football team have this good opportunity, which is an unprecedented event.

Local News

The Public Works Department and Shanghai Telephone Company

Sign a Franchise Contract

A Total of Twenty-Nine Clauses

The Shanghai Telephone Company, organized by the International Telephone and Telegraph Company, has purchased the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company. After the Board of Directors of the Public Works Department of the International Settlement approved the move, the Public Works Department signed a franchise contract with the representatives of the Shanghai Telephone Company yesterday. The contract contains a total of twenty-nine clauses, the main points of which are as follows:

(Clause 1) Definitions: In this contract, the term "settlement" includes all governed territorial boundaries, roads built outside the boundary, and land under management. The term "Public Works Department" refers to the existing Public Works Department and its successors. (Clause 2) Recognition of License: The Public Works Department recognizes that the company inherits the interests of the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company and enjoys all original rights of the Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company. (Clause 3) Franchise: The Public Works Department allows the company to enjoy the telephone franchise in the settlement and only allows the company to excavate roads and land, bury cables, and erect poles after the Public Works Department has approved them. (Clause 4) Supplementary Business: The company may start or suspend supplementary businesses related to telephones at any time, but must first obtain the approval of the Public Works Department. The Public Works Department may separately formulate special articles to manage them, and this supplementary business shall not hinder the effectiveness of the telephone and shall not force telephone users to purchase it. The company shall not enjoy exclusive rights for supplementary businesses. (Clause 5) Effectiveness: The company shall maintain first-class service. If the Public Works Department believes that the company has failed to fulfill the obligations stipulated in this contract, it may immediately submit to arbitration. If the company still fails to fulfill the arbitration result after twelve months, the Public Works Department may terminate the contract and cancel the franchise by written notice. (Clause 6) Promotion: If the company installs telephones outside the settlement, it must first obtain the consent of the Public Works Department. (Clause 7) Road Excavation Rights: When the company excavates roads and land managed by the Public Works Department, it shall work in the fastest possible way. After the work is completed, it shall fill the roads and land in the same quick way and remove the remaining soil and rocks. The Public Works Department shall be responsible for re-paving the roads, and the company shall pay the expenses. (Clause 8) Road Excavation: If the Public Works Department excavates roads and ditches when necessary, which hinders the company's work or services, or if any individual or company uses roads or Public Works Department land with the approval of the Public Works Department, which hinders the company's work or services, the company shall not claim damages from the Public Works Department. However, damage to or cutting off the company's aerial lines, underground lines, and telephone poles are not included. (Clause 9) The telephone company's telephone poles and other visible equipment should be kept neat and beautiful as far as reasonably possible and kept in good condition. Advertising shall not be hung or posted without the permission of the Public Works Department. (Clause 10) Obstruction of Other Businesses: If a lawsuit for damages is filed due to the company's negligence or fault in construction or operation, the company shall be responsible for the compensation and shall not cause the Public Works Department to suffer any loss. (Clause 11) Aerial Wires: Aerial wires shall not exceed six hundred and fifty pairs, of which bare wires shall not exceed ten pairs, and the total of bare wires and sheathed wires shall not exceed one hundred pairs. The rest must use cables, but aerial cables shall not exceed three. If the Public Works Department believes that any aerial cable needs to be changed to underground, the company shall do so within twelve months after receiving the notice. (Clause 12) Municipal Regulations: Unless otherwise stipulated, the clauses listed in this contract shall not restrict the powers and rights of the Public Works Department in accordance with the Yangjingbang Regulations and the attached laws. (Clause 13) The current tariff regulations in effect on the date of implementation of this contract shall remain in effect until the completion of the project to convert to automatic machines. However, the shareholder discount shall be cancelled. The tariff regulations after the completion of the conversion to automatic machines shall be agreed upon by the company and the Public Works Department based on a net profit of 8% per year on the capital invested in the business, plus an additional 2%. If the company cannot complete the conversion to automatic machines within two years as stipulated in Clause 27, the fee can only be increased after a period equal to twice the number of days of the delay. (Clause 14) Revision of Tariff Regulations: The tariff regulations may be negotiated and stipulated by the company, the Public Works Department, and the French Municipal Council from time to time, but not more than once a year. If the company can prove that the annual net profit is less than 8% plus 2% due to an accident and is satisfied by the Public Works Department, the fee may be increased. If the annual net profit exceeds this number, the fee shall be reduced. The company shall not agree on any measures regarding the revision of tariff regulations or the implementation of new regulations based on the number of calls made, or affecting the common interests of users of the Public Works Department, the French Municipal Council, the French Concession, and the Public Settlement, without the agreement of the above two municipal governments. (Clause 15) Public Reserve Fund: The 2% annual net profit mentioned in Clause 13 shall be used as a public reserve fund. (Clause 16) Excess Profit and Revision of Tariff Regulations: If the company's annual net profit exceeds the prescribed amount, 50% of the excess amount shall be used as the company's additional profit, and the remaining 50% shall be used to revise the tariff regulations. If the net profit is less than the prescribed amount due to an accident, the deficiency shall be made up by allocating the revision of the tariff regulations. (Clause 17) Increasing Capital and Establishing Borrowing Rights: The company may increase the capital necessary to implement its procedures and develop its business. The company shall freely decide on the behavior of raising necessary capital. The company shall consult with the Public Works Department and the French Municipal Council on the details of its general development procedures and annual development. The company shall give appropriate consideration to any suggestions from the two municipal governments on this matter. (Clause 18) Taxes and Discounts: The telephone fee paid by the Public Works Department to the company during the term of this contract shall be reduced by 20% of the total amount. The company shall pay 2% of the gross amount of fees collected in the Public Settlement in accordance with this contract in the second five years of this contract, and 4% in the following ten years. (Clause 19) Transfer of Franchise: The rights and special benefits enjoyed by the company in accordance with this contract may not be transferred without the written permission of the Public Works Department. (Clause 20) No Exclusive Rights Granted: Except for the rights expressly stipulated in this contract, the clauses contained in the contract shall not be interpreted as the Public Works Department, etc., having granted the company exclusive rights. (Clause 21) Termination Right: If the company is unable to comply with the provisions of Clause 5 at any time, or if the company is unable to maintain its system of continuous operation for 31 days, except for the special reasons stipulated in Clause 28, the Public Works Department may terminate this contract immediately by written notice. The company's property within the Public Works Department may be retained by the Public Works Department as collateral pending resolution of the legal claims made by the Public Works Department against the company. If this legal claim cannot be resolved within two months after the termination of this contract, the Public Works Department may sell or dispose of the above-mentioned collateral property to offset the claim. (Clause 22) Regarding the supply of telephones to users and the regulations to be observed by users, the regulations shall be submitted to the Public Works Department for approval before they can be implemented. (Clause 23) Regarding the supply of telephones to the police department, fire alarm, and barracks. (Clause 24) All work carried out by the company on the roads or land of the Public Works Department and on the roads or land under the jurisdiction of the Public Works Department shall be supervised by the Public Works Department and approved by the Public Works Department and its staff. (Clause 25) The Public Works Department may inspect the company's books at appropriate times. (Clause 26) Franchise Period and Public Works Department's Right of Purchase: This contract shall take effect on August 5, 1930, and shall be valid for forty years. If the Public Works Department does not notify of the purchase two years before the expiration, it shall continue to be valid, but thereafter it shall be for a period of ten years. When the Public Works Department notifies of the purchase, the company must sell it to the Public Works Department at a price agreed upon by consent. If the price cannot be agreed upon, it shall be submitted to arbitration. (Clause 27) Penalties: The company shall convert all telephones to automatic machines within two years after the signing of the contract. If it fails to complete the installation by the deadline, it may increase the telephone fee only after the installation is completed and after a period equal to twice the number of days of the delay. (Clause 28) Natural Disasters and Man-made Disasters: If the company or the Public Works Department is unable to complete the obligations stipulated in this contract as scheduled due to natural disasters, man-made disasters, or uncontrollable circumstances, they shall be excused. (Clause 29) Arbitration: If the contracting parties have any doubts or questions regarding construction, or the meaning and effect of this contract, or the rights and obligations of both parties, each party shall appoint two unrelated persons to submit to arbitration. The two arbitrators shall appoint a third arbitrator in writing before the arbitration. If the arbitrators cannot agree on the judgment, they shall submit it to the third arbitrator for review. If one of the arbitrators requests the appointment of a third arbitrator and the other arbitrator fails to agree within seven days, the British Consul General in Shanghai shall be requested to appoint the first arbitrator. Also, if one party appoints an arbitrator and notifies the other party, and the other party fails to appoint an arbitrator within thirty days, the appointed arbitrator shall make a judgment independently based on the request of the appointer. The contracting parties agree that a lawsuit shall not be filed unless one party refuses arbitration or does not comply with the arbitration result. When filing a lawsuit, the company declares that it is subject to the jurisdiction of the United States Consulate General in Shanghai or other courts that have jurisdiction over American expatriates in Shanghai at that time.

Hurricane Outside Wusongkou Last Night

Coastal Dikes Were Destroyed

Waves Rushed In

A hurricane suddenly arose outside Wusongkou last night, and it was quite fierce. The coastal dikes of Shitou Sha and Dingxing Sha were destroyed by the turbid waves, causing houses and sheds in the vicinity to collapse and all objects to float in all directions. Men, women, old and young, fled in succession, and the cries were deafening. The tide began to recede at dawn yesterday, but the losses were huge. Yesterday, the public groups of these sands discussed relief measures to reassure the people.

Ma Hongkui Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Ma Hongkui, the commander-in-chief of the 15th Route Army, arrived in Shanghai yesterday at 5:30 PM on the Fengtian Maru from Qingdao. Accompanying him were Secretary-General Feng Dingcheng, Councilor Qiu Jiecun, Yao Ruilin, and more than a dozen others. A reporter from Guowen News Agency went to the residence to interview Mr. Ma. He was suffering from a headache and abdominal pain due to the heat along the way and had already sought medical treatment. He received the reporter with difficulty. He said that this trip was to inspect the direct troops along the Jiaoji Railway Line. He himself had gone to Gaomi, where Commander-in-Chief Han Xiangfang (Fu Ju) was stationed. The advance troops had already advanced and surrounded Zhucheng. He did not know when he would go to Beijing. On the table was a telegram from the headquarters of the 15th Route Army sent from Yanzhou at 7:00 PM on the 4th, reporting the military situation on the Jinpu Railway Line. Mr. Ma agreed to give a copy to the reporter and said that everything could be known from this. The reporter, thinking that Commander Ma needed to rest, then bid farewell. The original telegram is as follows: (1) No changes on the Longhai and Pinghan lines. (2) The right-wing army of the Jinpu line has arrived in the vicinity of Tai'an. The enemy in the Xiemating area of Ningyang has been defeated and is retreating north. The Central Army is pursuing in the vicinity of Tai'an from Nanyi. One unit has reached the northeast of Feicheng, and another unit has reached the Jieshou area northwest of Tai'an. (3) The left-wing army is pursuing towards Dongping.

Also, a copper seal for the Secretariat of the Municipal Government reads: Shanghai Municipal Government Secretariat, etc." Accordingly, the letter is sent for your review and forwarding for collection and use, and you are instructed to submit the date of commencement of use to this government for reference, and to destroy the old seals by cutting off the corners.
