Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Seafarer

Daughter—Mother, my younger sister swallowed a silver coin!

Mother—Why weren't you careful? What should we do, what should we do?

Daughter—I think it's better to swallow a button to button up that coin.

A—My friend, please help me. My wife has already given birth to three daughters, and now she's had twins. I'm always spending more than I earn every month. I'm so tired!

B—How old are your twins?

A—One is seven weeks old, and the other is eight months old.

A—Why did you put a big mirror on the bed?

B—I like to look in the mirror the most. Since there's a mirror on the bed, I can see if my face after I fall asleep is as beautiful as it is during the day.

Girl—Why do you always walk so far away and don't want to be with me every night when we go out for a walk?

Boy—Because I respect and love you so much that I'm afraid of stepping on your shadow if I get too close.

A—The military officer has gone to another place with the army. Did he pay for the cloth he bought from your store on credit?

B—No, I knew I should have raised the price of the cloth by one or two times.

A Brief Stay at Mogan Mountain (4)

— Jingbo

The famous scenic spots in the mountains can be visited almost entirely if one plans the itinerary by day. However, climbing the mountains to escape the summer heat should be done with leisure and pleasure. Following where the spirit takes you, taking a leisurely stroll with a walking stick, there is no need to rush to every mountain peak and generate startling sweat. I stayed in the mountains for several days, living quietly in the lodge. The bamboo shadows fill the steps, and the rich greenery pleases the eye. Looking out the window at a corner of the green mountains, this small amount of pure pleasure is enough. The corridor on the upper floor of the railway hotel is very wide. The sofas and other furnishings are neatly arranged. After dinner, I sit for a while, and the mountain breeze blows continuously. The joy is infinite. From the high eastern terrace, I can look down on the mountains as if they are under my feet. The winding road from Sanqiaobu to Yucun is like a long snake, also leisurely in sight. The day after climbing the mountain, mountain rain was about to come. Clouds and fog filled the sky, a vast expanse. The mountains suddenly disappeared. Standing in the precarious building, it was as if I were on a ship sailing rapidly in the vast ocean. After a while, the rain stopped, and white clouds flew like tattered cotton. The mountain scenery also changed unpredictably, sometimes hidden, sometimes visible, sometimes bright, sometimes dim. When the clouds cleared, the bamboo shadows and mountain mist rushed to the eyebrows again. The changes between sunny and rainy days are instantaneous. I sigh at the sight.

Mogan Mountain has ten mountains, such as Pao Tai Mountain, Shangheng Mountain, Yin Mountain, Gangtou Mountain, Gangtou Dun, Zhonghua Mountain, Luhua Dang, Jinjia Mountain, Mantou Mountain, and Ta Mountain. Pao Tai Mountain is the gateway to the mountains via the old road. Shangheng Mountain has a small market. Yin Mountain is the most prosperous place in Mogan Mountain because its terrain is flat and it is located in the center of the mountains, making transportation convenient. Lodges, banks, bookstores, and shops in the mountains are all clustered here. The old church is also in Yin Mountain. Now that the new church is completed, the Westerners have sold the site of the old church to the Shanghai Bank and the Commercial Press. The time for the transfer of the house is next year. This is also a small vicissitude in the mountains.

A Collection of Strange Tales from Mingguang

— Jiefei

The Last Life and Death: A Mr. Wang lives a few dozen miles from the town, earning a living as an old gardener. His nephew was studious and hardworking when he was young. When he grew up, he became a monk, wearing straw sandals and carrying a begging bowl, visiting various mountains. Recently, he traveled north to Mount Wutai and returned to visit his uncle. That evening, he fell seriously ill. The uncle hurriedly bought a thin coffin in the market. When the coffin arrived, the monk recovered. The uncle was sick and dying, so he was placed in the coffin.

Airplane Sight Becomes Blindness: Zhang Da Duzi, who lives east of the town and makes a living by gardening, is known to everyone as an old and sincere person. He first came to Mingguang alone and worked hard. Now his children and grandchildren are around his knees, and the onions and chives fill the ridges. Although he is eighty years old, he is still healthy. A few days ago, a national army airplane flew north along the Jinpu Line. In the shadow of the clouds, Zhang Lao's eyes were dim. He stared at the clouds and suddenly fell to the ground and died. It can be said that he was blinded by one sight.

Three Women Give Birth to Eight Children: Near the north street of the town, three women gave birth to eight children one night: two boys and one girl, one two girls and one boy, and one one boy and one girl. The news spread quickly, and women from all over the town formed teams to watch, calling it a miracle.

A Visit to the Battlefield

— Ji Ya

If one is on the battlefield, bathed in blood and the stench of war every day, and does not personally go to the front line to witness the situation, how can one know how those with broken arms and pierced chests came to be? Wouldn't that be a great regret? I have had this ambition for a long time, but I have never had the opportunity. I met Zhao Guantao, the commander of the Sixth Division, who wanted to go to the front line to observe the position. The day before, he sent his adjutant, Xu Shipu, to ask if I would like to go. I immediately said yes. The division headquarters was about ten miles away from the front line. Two trucks were taken, one for the officers and one for the guards. They drove quickly in the green gauze tent, and the dust covered the eyes, making it impossible to see the sky. In an instant, the car stopped, and they got out of the car and walked to the regimental headquarters of the 35th Regiment for a short rest, slightly eating melons and plums to relieve the heat. Then they divided into teams to go, because they were afraid that a large group of people would be shelled by the enemy. After walking less than a mile, short walls were arranged horizontally like the Great Wall. Commander Zhao said that this was a defensive work. The wall was built with earth, only as high as a person and about three feet thick. Under the wall was a deep ditch, with an outer trench on the outside and a communication trench on the inside. About ten steps outside the trench, there was barbed wire and two rows of wooden stakes, with the wire wrapped around like a net. At intervals of a few steps between the nets, there was a kerosene bag, and a sentry was assigned to guard it. If the enemy approached, the sentry would light the kerosene bag, illuminating it as if it were daytime, and the guard could use it to aim and shoot. There was an underground room in the ditch for the guards to rest in shifts. It was high enough to stand upright and wide enough to lie down. Wood was erected above to support the earth, level with the ground, so it was not easily invaded by artillery fire. Residents near the front line often imitated this to avoid danger. The side of the village's houses facing the enemy was regarded as a natural fortress, with holes pierced in the walls as gun holes and walls broken to make doors for easy transportation. If the enemy broke through the barbed wire and attacked the outer trench, there were also field bunkers for flanking attacks. The shape of the bunker was like an underground room, with gun holes all around, located between the outer trenches, and could be fired in all directions. With such deep trenches and high walls, even if the attackers suffered great sacrifices, they would not be able to do anything. Ji Hongchang's troops were the elite of Feng's troops, known for their bravery. They had repeatedly launched fierce attacks, but so far almost all of them had been killed or injured. There was even a mutual warning not to invade the Sixth Division's defense zone, and the Sixth Division's strict defense was as solid as ever. While visiting, a bullet came from the enemy and landed without exploding about a hundred steps away from us. The bullet weighed about sixty or seventy pounds. Commander Zhao said that this was a heavy mortar, and its explosive power was very strong. I said that if it had exploded, we would all have been crushed to pieces, and I couldn't help but feel frightened. Before long, the sound of crackling sounded like a string of beads, as if we were the target. A certain company commander's hat brim was suddenly pierced by a bullet, and it almost hit the top of his head. The enemy was less than a mile away from the position. If there were no sorghum stalks to separate them, their movements would be clear to each other, and those nearby could even hear their laughter. According to the sentries, the enemy often used tricks to confuse people, sometimes setting off firecrackers, red and green, in front of the position, or holding large lantern parties inside the defense zone. Sometimes they raised their voices and shouted, "Folks, we have no pay, we are starving and freezing, we really can't stand the hardship. We are willing to surrender." Although their words were sweet, their hearts were very cunning, and they were never moved by them. The Sixth Division's defense zone was almost thirty miles long. What I observed that day was less than one-fifth. Although I didn't get to see the whole picture, I could infer the rest from what I saw. This trip was with Zhao Guantao, Chief of Staff Zhou Bi Yan, 17th Brigade Commander Fan Songfu, 18th Brigade Commander Chen Shiji, and various regimental and battalion commanders of the Sixth Division.

A New Invention of a Car Trailer

— Chuan San Cao Tong

The number of cars in the world is increasing every day, and the roads in Zhejiang are the most developed area in China. The yellow sand roads are winding and endless, extending in all directions, almost all over the territory, making transportation extremely convenient. The recently built lines, in addition to the Beijing-Hangzhou Road, such as the Hang-Chang, Hang-Ping, and Hang-Hu lines in this province, have all been opened to traffic one after another. Therefore, the Road Bureau recently needs to purchase a large number of public cars for application. However, due to the soaring price of gold and the surge in foreign goods, the price of these cars has also increased. Therefore, Mr. Wu Zhuozhi, the chief of the car service of the bureau, carefully planned and invented a car trailer in the shortest possible time. It is economical and can carry more passengers and luggage. It is truly rare in the world. Moreover, the car body is stable, flexible, and extremely easy to tow without any hindrance. A few days ago, Chairman Zhang of the provincial government and his wife personally test-drove the car, passing through Hubin, Guanxiang, Baoyoufang, and the Sanlang Temple section. At that time, the onlookers along the way were very crowded, and everyone marveled. Although the scorching sun was like fire, the car had already left, but the onlookers were still reluctant to leave, all looking up and wanting to chase after it, because it was an unprecedented creation.

As for the structure of the car, except for the tires, axles, and certain parts, the rest are self-made, so it is exceptionally economical. It costs about 1,000 yuan to make one, which saves a lot compared to buying foreign goods. Since the invention of this car, it can also reduce the cost of drivers and gasoline when driving on the highway. It is now heard that Chairman Zhang has ordered the bureau to rush to make more vehicles and use the Gongsan section as a test site. It is expected that after the completion of the trial, the results will be satisfactory, and the world will imitate it, making travel convenient and bringing happiness to the people.

Heart Shadows of Eastern Travel (25)

— Qian Hua

In terms of transportation, tram lines are popular all over the city, and the fare is seven cents for a one-way trip and one dime and three cents for a round trip, regardless of distance, and can be accessed everywhere. Public buses charge one dime for a one-way trip. In addition, there are long-distance trams traveling to various parts of Tokyo Prefecture. They depart every five minutes from the station, and the fare starts from one dime, depending on the distance. Families in the middle and lower classes find housing prices in Tokyo City expensive, so they live in Tokyo Prefecture and commute by long-distance tram. It takes more than ten minutes and there is no inconvenience. In the morning and evening, long-distance trams are extremely crowded, as residents of Tokyo Prefecture come and go. For the sake of embellishing civilization, Tokyo City built an underground railway from Asakusa to Manseibashi, with a total of four stations. It was opened to traffic on January 1st of this year. The fare is one dime. It is safe, fast, and convenient for travelers. There are very few rickshaws, which have been naturally eliminated. Travelers from afar who do not know the streets find it difficult to take trams and have to hire cars. The fare in the city is one yuan per day for a one-way trip, and two dimes are added for each additional person, so the car fare is especially expensive every day. There are 13,968 cars in Tokyo City, and 70% of them are commercial vehicles. Most of the rickshaw pullers of the past have changed their ways and learned to drive cars. After learning, they either rent from car companies or borrow money at high interest rates to buy cars. The average daily income is about forty or fifty yuan. After deducting gasoline, rent, and other items, the net profit is about twenty yuan per day. The monthly income is six hundred yuan. The grooms are usually their children and nephews, and their salaries are only a little decoration, which is especially economical. Therefore, the car driver is the most popular occupation in Tokyo's labor force. Most of the commercial vehicles are new-style sedans, luxurious and magnificent, no different from the consulate's cars. Some old covered cars can be ridden for five dimes for a one-way trip. Most of the car drivers hired by car companies are poor Koreans, otherwise, those who are slightly able would not bother to do it. Simple cafeterias are the only restaurants for ordinary people. They are everywhere in the streets, and the interior is very clean. Most of the meals are set meals. The so-called set meal is a fixed dish and rice that cannot be changed. The breakfast is usually two dimes, including soup, pickles, rice, and a small bucket. Lunch is divided into five dimes and three dimes, including a fish, a vegetable, and a soup. Dinner is the same as lunch. If the rice is not enough, you can add a little. In addition, there are noodles, etc., for one or two dimes per bowl. Students, workers, and others all eat here, and the business is extremely developed. They are also supervised by the health police, who often come to check. The reporter has eaten there several times with friends, and the taste is extremely clean and delicious. It is truly the most economical restaurant in Japan. Most of the Chinese students in our country, except for a small part who eat at the Chinese Youth Association in Kanda District (the Youth Association has Chinese cooks who provide meals for four dimes per meal), also use simple cafeterias for their meals. The dormitories are all in Tokyo Prefecture, and the room fee is about ten yen per month. Usually, the most frugal students need fifty yen per month, which is equivalent to one hundred yuan in national currency, which is really difficult to make a living. This time, the players from our country stayed at the Japan Youth Hall, and the laundry and other matters were handled by the laundry company at a special discount. Washing a pair of socks cost one dime, a shirt cost four dimes, and a pair of white twill cloth suit pants cost one yuan. The representatives were speechless. In order to save money, the coaches told the players to wash the small items themselves, but the laundry expenses were still very considerable. Also, the four Indian players who went to Japan for the first time stayed in Shanghai for a short time. When the reporter visited them, they said that the prices in Shanghai were the cheapest, and the food and accommodation were extremely comfortable. Compared with Tokyo today, there is a world of difference. The life in Tokyo can be seen in a glimpse.

Warmth in the Heart (248)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Thirteen: Who Unintentionally Sows Fortune and Gets a Diamond Ring? Only This Fate Has the Heart to Sing of Golden Threads

Zuo Shichen said that was very good. Although I don't understand calligraphy, painting, or antiques, you should also buy a few tickets when you issue that kind of lottery ticket. Shi Guanping smiled and said, "Have you tasted the sweetness? You should buy more of our lottery tickets. To say something superstitious, your luck is very good. Taking advantage of this time of good luck, you won a second prize with the fortune ticket. Who knows, maybe you will win a first prize with our lottery ticket? All things that are close to gambling depend on luck. Let's take the most superficial game of mahjong as an example. If you are in good luck, even if you are a novice, you will win with a big hand, isn't there a saying in Suzhou that says, 'Even a novice can win with a good hand'? If you are in bad luck, even if you are an expert, luck will go against you. You yourself listen to the three, six, and nine bamboos and you can't win a peaceful hand, but the upstream family covers the six bamboos and wins. Then it becomes 'A robber fights a lawsuit and always loses.' At that time, you can only avoid the wind and be sensible. You are in very good luck now, so you can buy more tickets. After the tickets are printed, I will distribute them to you." Zuo Shichen said, "I suspect that the fruits and melons you donate are not very good things, but broken copper and rotten iron. Although I am an outsider and don't understand calligraphy, painting, or antiques, I have seen those collectors and antique dealers, and they are reluctant to show off a fine piece easily. When people want to see it, they always procrastinate. How can they be willing to part with it and donate it to the charity association?" Shi Guanping said, "You are right about that. Many collectors have this habit. They think they have a secret to themselves when they have a good thing, and they won't even let people take a look at it, as if they have married a beautiful concubine. They keep her hidden in a golden house and lock her in a jade pass. But now that things are more open, even if they have married a beautiful concubine, they often take her out to show off. There is no such thing as keeping her deeply hidden. But some people have such a temperament, and it is impossible to force them. However, collectors also have a kind of suffering. I think that if they encounter a generation of knowledgeable connoisseurs, collectors are extremely welcome. There is no way that they would not be willing to let them see their things. Moreover, they are honored by having a certain connoisseur look over their calligraphy and paintings, and they also ask him to write inscriptions. For other antiques, they also ask him to do research. But if they encounter that kind of fake connoisseur, who doesn't understand anything himself, but wants to blindly criticize others, saying that you are fake when it is indeed genuine, and after seeing it, he will spread rumors and spread rumors outside, no collector is willing to let him see it. Moreover, antiques can be explained to the knowledgeable, but it is difficult to explain them to ordinary people. Therefore, antiques are called antiques, and those who don't understand will always be separated. Furthermore, those antiques are probably not able to endure much suffering. There is no benefit in letting too many irrelevant people see them, not to mention the damage."

Commercial News

Finance

Gold Market Softens

Psychological Anxiety, Market Shape Hesitant, Finally Retreats

Yesterday, the attitude of the gold market on the 5th was secretly sluggish, but it contained unpredictable fluctuations. It was firm in the morning, tired at noon, and mediocre in the afternoon. The range of the daily fluctuations totaled nine taels, and it broke the 80 taels level again. As for the exchange rate, it remained stable. There were no large transactions in the market. The psychology of various dealers was hesitant, sometimes buying and sometimes selling. Zhifeng, Yongyuan, Xingyong, etc. all bought in, while Yuancheng, Yongheng, Yuancheng, Yongxiang, Yuwansheng, etc. mostly sold out. In the morning market, the previous day's large contract was reduced, and it opened high. Afterwards, the sellers were active and turned downward, but there were occasional swings of two or three taels. The trend at noon was weak. From morning to noon, it almost fell by ten taels. Later, Hengxing, Zhifeng, Yong, etc. fluctuated, and Yuanxing, Yongheng, Wanxing, etc. sold out. And the price had a slight rotation, but there were only three taels of expansion and contraction. The exchange rate was flat. Finally, it was considered to be around 77 taels. Yesterday, there was no electricity for the large contract, but the market had shrunk by one-eighth on Sunday (3rd), and the silver price had also shrunk by one-eighth. The exchange rate did not change.

The Opening Was Still Pretty, but Later There Was a Big Setback

The opening price of gold in September increased by two taels and one qian to 82 taels and seven qian for the gross price. It had been to 84 taels and five qian and then retreated to within 82 taels because the buying and selling were equal, the market situation was divided. Yarn and Cotton Market: Yarn Sales Exceptionally Strong

The standard market is becoming increasingly strong.

The actual sales of cotton yarn are exceptionally brisk. The Cantonese merchants are becoming increasingly eager to collect supplies. The Xuzhou and Yunnan merchants are following suit, but mostly buying futures. The main reason is that this year's harvest is expected to be abundant, and there will definitely be a large demand in the future. Therefore, various merchants are taking precautions. The coarse yarn from several factories for October, November, and December has already been purchased, and the Japanese yarn for February and March of next year has all been sold. Therefore, the current market situation is extremely strong. The amount of goods dragged in by fellow merchants and customer merchants is very large. If spot sales do not go smoothly in the future, there will be drastic changes in the market. However, it is difficult for the current market price to fall, and the standard yarn for 10-count coarse yarn is becoming increasingly tight. Therefore, buyers must watch for 60 taels for customs clearance.

Vermicelli Consistently and Wildly Rises Near and Far

Foreign wheat rises rapidly... Existing stocks are weak... Sharp increase of more than four fen

After the opening of the vermicelli market yesterday morning, the prices for various months continued to rise sharply. Due to the rapid increase in the price of foreign wheat by 1.12 yuan to 1.14 yuan, people's hearts were agitated. The opening price was immediately raised by about 1.5 fen compared to the previous day. Afterwards, as major factories became increasingly reluctant to sell and off-market short sellers also aggressively covered their positions, and it was rumored that Tianjin would ship wheat to the Yangtze River area, but before the political situation was settled, there would be no smooth arrival, so near-term was tight due to inventory, while far-term increased wildly due to foreign wheat. Although small and medium-sized factories still took advantage of the situation to offer goods, the buying sentiment was strong, so the more they sold, the higher the price rose. If the factory's attitude does not change in the future, and if the timing is right, the upward trend is still considerable. As a result, August, September, and January rose by 3.75 fen each compared to the previous day, and October to December rose by 4.5 fen each.

Wheat Futures Continue to Soar

Spot goods are scarce and also good at 3-4 fen

The wheat futures market yesterday showed a consistent and sharp increase in the market for all months in the morning and afternoon. The reason for this was initially that the increase in foreign wheat prices stimulated the hearts of most people. Fundamentally speaking, the current stock of wheat is only about 50,000 bags, and most of them are of medium quality, with very few high-quality goods. Furthermore, the domestic shipping price has not been greatly reduced, and most hoarding households, due to the relationship of the purchase price, are unwilling to sell unless they hold to the target price. Therefore, the future of the exchange's standards is very worthy of consideration by operators. Due to this situation, the near-term is good, but the far-term is even better. As a result, this month rose by 7 fen compared to the previous day, September rose by 8 fen, October rose by 9 fen, November rose by 8 fen, December rose by 1 qian, and January rose by 4 fen. The spot wheat market is good because the standard has soared again and the arriving goods are thin, so the opening price of each grade is good at 3-4 fen. It is reported that Fuxin has bought more than 5,000 bags of wheat from Yaowan, Suqian, Jiangxi, Shantou, and Hankou.

Silk, Tea, and Dried Cocoons: Daily Sales Stagnant

After our country's new cocoons are on the market, Japanese firms in recent years have been purchasing dried cocoons from Jiangsu and Zhejiang and transporting them to Japan to supplement raw materials. This year, both our country's spring and summer cocoons have been in short supply, while Japan's harvest has been very abundant. Silk sales have been sluggish, and there is overproduction. In addition, our country's silk cocoon merchants have restricted the transportation of cocoons to Japan due to a lack of raw materials. Therefore, the daily sales of dried cocoons have been stagnant for a long time. In the past two months, no silkworm cocoons have been transported from our country to Japan.

American Firms' Silk Sales Quietly Await Telegrams

The transaction of futures silk by foreign firms in this port: The sales of American silk have begun to take action last weekend. As Chinese silk merchants believe that the price of silk is not cheap and European firms' opening prices are not high, the result of the negotiations is that the booking can only be completed after receiving a telegram from overseas. It remains to be seen. Yesterday, only Velon, etc., took in 20 packages of Shanghai white factory silk, and Samsung, etc., took in 15 packages of yellow coarse silk. The prices were all firm.

Land Firms' Tea Arrivals: Over 140,000 Cases

Land firms' green tea is produced from Wuyuan, Tunxi, Shexian, Suian, Dexing, and various other routes. It is also an important commodity in the foreign firms' tea market. Last year's output was estimated at over 320,000 cases. The number of teas from various routes this year has been greatly reduced. The reason for this is that the sales in the Shanghai market have been greatly sluggish, and the tea-making firms have taken a cautious approach and have stopped purchasing goods one after another. In the tea-producing areas, no one has been harvesting summer tea, and most of the spring tea has been sold as grain. Currently, the amount of land firms' tea that has arrived at various tea shops is two-thirds of the total, and the estimated amount is no more than 140,000 cases. The survey is divided as follows: Hongyuan Yong 26,833 cases, Shenyuan 19,820 cases, Yongshengchang 19,409 cases, Yuanfengrun 17,197 cases, Gong Shengyong 16,804 cases, Shengchang Sheng 11,427 cases, Yongxinglong 10,198 cases, Zhongxin Chang 8,816 cases, Rende Yong 4,732 cases, Yuancheng Yong 3,822 cases, Qianji 1,286 cases, for a total of 140,344 cases.

18-gauge black iron sheets are a crucial necessity for winter. Northern firms inevitably purchase them during the summer and autumn. Large quantities have already been purchased in the previous week. It is reported that this is the second transaction, with the number of transactions reaching 8-900 bundles. It is found that the Liaodong and Tianjin firms purchased them. Although there were inquiries from Beiping and Qingdao, the actual transactions were limited. It is assumed that they also have orders locally. The price per bundle (100 pounds) is 11.5 taels. In addition, due to the favorable trend of 18-gauge sheets, 3-gauge to 13-gauge sheets with a size of 36 inches are also selling well, with a price of 9.3-4 taels.

North-South Goods: New Golden Lily Buds are Already Cheap and Suitable

Prevent price increase later

Since the release of new golden needle vegetables, there have been quite a few arrivals before and after, and the stocks on the market are also thick. Therefore, the market price has gradually turned down, reaching as much as four or five taels. However, the trend seems to have reached a considerable level at this point, and it is now gradually stabilizing. Therefore, the purchases of various helpers have become lively again, and the number of plates are also being opened one after another. Ordinary goods are not more than twenty taels, which can be said to be extremely cheap. If the price increases again in the market, it will inevitably increase.

Shanghai Market

Theater News

The Star Film Company announces that its director Zheng Zhengqiu is skilled at creating delicate and poignant works, and that his recent films have made immeasurable contributions in the area of emotions, further enhancing his reputation. The "Peach Blossom Lake," which he wrote and directed, has even deeper contributions. Filming is nearing completion, and the Peach Blossom Lake scene was filmed yesterday. Originally, it was intended to be filmed using natural scenery, but after considering the angle of photography, the position of the filming, and the beauty of the light, it was deemed more appropriate to use artificial sets. Therefore, the company's set design and art departments collaborated to set up the scene at the outdoor filming location. The lake area is very large, and hundreds of peach trees are decorated with bright and vibrant peach blossoms, shining brilliantly and reflecting the light of the lake water, creating extreme beauty. Coupled with soft and pleasing electric lights, the actors in the play, Hu Die, Xia Peizhen, and Zheng Xiaoqiu, produce a supreme beautifying effect. This set, along with the original Kulun snow scene and the modernly decorated Miss's bedroom and the luxurious piano room, are rare scenes in the development of domestic films.

Publishing News

The Buddhist Bookstore at the Baoshan Road intersection announces that its specialization in compiling and publishing Buddhist books and newspapers has long been welcomed by all sectors. Now, it has compiled a Buddhist series called "Hai Chao Yin Wen Ku" (Ocean Tide Sound Library), which is edited from the "Hai Chao Yin" monthly magazine over the past decade. The complete set consists of thirty-four volumes, scheduled to be published successively starting this October. Pre-orders will be accepted until the end of September this year. Those who wish to know more details and samples can write to the bookstore.

The Guochan Daobao (Domestic Products Guide) announces that the newspaper is organized by Cao Chi Gong, Zhang Yizai, and others, dedicated to promoting domestic products as its main purpose. The inaugural issue was published last week and has been well received by all sectors. The second issue will be published today with rich content and lively writing, combining seriousness and humor. An annex, "Chenlie Guan" (Exhibition Hall), edited by Jin Da Gui (Cai Xiaohe), is also witty and interesting. In order to devote itself to the promotion of domestic goods, the newspaper vows to sacrifice by only charging postage for those who request it, whether local or out of town (one cent for local, two cents for out of town), without charging for the newspaper itself. The address of the exhibition hall is No. 2136, Hongxiang Li, Xinzha Road.

The Lao Tong Shun Chang felt and carpet store on South Jixiang Street in the French Concession announces that the water-shedding medicine and dysentery pills produced by this store are indeed miraculously effective in treating diarrhea and dysentery. Regardless of men, women, old, or young, once taken, they are effective as if by magic. Therefore, for more than eighty years, countless people have been cured. The summer and autumn seasons are precisely when this disease is prevalent. If this medicine is administered, the disease will be eliminated and the pain relieved. It is truly a good medicine for diarrhea and dysentery.

Automobile News

Special Article

Newly Invented Automobile Trailer

— Zhi Zheng

With Kitchen, Bedroom, and Dining Room

There is no doubt that the automobile industry is progressing and developing soundly. However, it is never easy to satisfy inventors, no matter how much they invent. For example, the current automobiles are not suitable for long-distance travel. Why? Because the space inside is too small; one cannot cook or sleep. Isn't this a very obvious shortcoming? In order to solve this problem, a new invention has been made. What is it? It is a trailer attached to the back of the car (as shown in the picture). The manufacturer is the Didjilao Auto Company, and the value is $385.

This trailer is six and a half feet wide, nine feet long, and six feet four inches high. The interior layout combines a kitchen and a bedroom. The body is made of solid wood, but the chassis is made of sturdy steel plates. The wooden boards on the four walls have the function of regulating the climate. In winter, it can ward off the cold, and in summer, it can keep out the heat. In winter, there is also a gasoline stove for heating. This type of car is most suitable for hunters. The top of the trailer is made of the same material as the top of the car. It is not afraid of rain and is not easily damaged. Moreover, a small boat can be placed on top. The weight of the entire trailer is only one-quarter of the weight of the car. It is very convenient for going uphill and at high speeds.

The detailed layout is roughly as follows: the bed is four feet wide and six feet long, with a window at each end. There are two refrigerators that can store 25 pounds of ice, and a water bucket with a capacity of five gallons, which not only provides drinking water but also is used for washing clothes and cooking. The electricity for the lights is supplied by a battery. The stove is a gasoline stove with two pots. A table can accommodate four people for dining and playing cards. Two chairs are also available for resting.

The interior layout is light blue and cream color. If other colors are desired, then an additional ten dollars will be charged. The advantage of this type of car is that it can alleviate the limitations of the general automobile. Long-distance travelers can cook their own meals when they are hungry and sleep peacefully at night. Although one is traveling, it is as comfortable as being at home. Currently, many people have purchased trailers, which can be easily detached.

Some people say that with a trailer, the speed will definitely decrease. However, this is not the case, because the bottom of the trailer is also connected to the engine of the front car, so the speed is not affected at all. It does not suffer major shocks when climbing hills, because it has a kind of spring to maintain balanced force.

Prerequisites for Developing Transportation

— Qu Zi

If we want to develop transportation in China today, building railways requires raising large sums of money and taking years to complete. If we talk about operating airlines, flight safety has not yet gained the trust of people, and the high price of tickets is beyond the means of most people in society. Therefore, neither of the two can be developed for the time being. Considering the situation, it is easier to build automobile roads.

I have investigated that the United States currently has an average of one mile of highway in every square mile of area. If one takes a public bus from San Francisco, one can cross the Americas and reach New York directly. The length of the road is about three thousand miles, and the accommodations and meals provided along the way are not inferior to those on a train. The road surface of this highway is extremely solid and extremely flat. The speed of the car is approximately 50 to 60 miles per hour continuously. The road administration also has buses and freight vehicles going to and from various villages to pick up passengers and take them to the railway trunk lines.

A Type of Road Building Machine from Gadby

Most of the roads in China have always been pedestrian paths, which can only accommodate small carts and rickshaws. If we want to allow the passage of buses and freight vehicles, then the weight of the vehicles themselves is already sufficient to damage the road surface, let alone carrying passengers and goods. Therefore, the highways that China needs today are exactly like those in the United States: they must be solid and flat, and convenient for drainage, so that they can be used in all seasons, and problems such as the speed of vehicles and the comfort of travelers will be solved easily.

Recently, Mr. Shi Waibo, the China representative of the California-based Gadby Motor Company, gave a speech at a luncheon at the Rotary Club of Shanghai last Thursday on the functions of the new Gadby road building machine. According to him, this road building machine only requires two workers and can build three miles of road per day. The cost of building one mile of road is only ten dollars. If road construction is done entirely by hand, the cost would be ten times higher than this. After the speech, a demonstration of the operation of this road building machine was shown on the Pingjin (Beijing-Tianjin) long-distance highway, showing its extremely skillful abilities to dig, plow, shovel, and roll. It is hereby introduced on the right, perhaps to the delight of those concerned with road construction.

Road Vehicle Management Issues

— Jia

In recent years, the number of automobiles has increased daily, and the method of managing their movement on the road has been the subject of much research. Professor MacDonald of political science at Benxifan University in the United States has written a book detailing the solution to this problem. Here are the main points as reference material for Shanghai's road administration.

The width of the road should be based on the amount of traffic on the road surface. The road should not be too narrow or too short. The traffic lights and various signs for management at road intersections should not be too small. The colors must be bright and the wording must be simple. The location must be conspicuous, and special attention should be paid at night, so that it can be recognized at a glance from far and near.

Widening the road surface is the only way to alleviate traffic congestion, but in prosperous streets, the land price is too expensive, and the cost of buying, selling, and reconstruction is too high. It is better to change to a longer aisle, that is, to incorporate the original pedestrian road into the road and, when building the house, to advance the second floor of the residence by six to ten feet as a pedestrian road, so that the area above the floor remains the same as the original area. (According to the road law, Dama Road has already imitated this style.)

Is the red and green light for traffic control harmful to the movement of automobiles? After much consideration by many experts, it is generally believed that if the green light suddenly changes to a red light, the car must stop immediately, and when the red light changes to a green light, the car must rush forward.

Page 26

Changing between red and green lights too quickly is prone to causing accidents. It is advocated to add an amber light between the red and green lights as a kind of preparatory signal. The timing of the lights is also a problem. The city of Detroit (the world's automobile industry base), which currently has the most automobiles, has recently been testing two new types of road traffic lights. Once they are effective, they will be implemented in various places. On busy streets, the most appropriate speed for cars is fifteen miles per hour. If it is too fast, the distance between cars will increase, and there is a deep fear that they will collide with each other, so the capacity of the road surface for vehicles cannot be fully utilized. Outside the city, where there are fewer vehicles, the speed can be increased. In busy cities, only fifteen miles per hour is allowed.

Parking lots occupy the most road surface. One of the most difficult things to solve in managing automobiles in large cities is the length of parking time, which varies depending on the local situation. Sometimes the road surface is insufficient. Large factories and large stores should automatically provide parking spaces for employees. However, shops on busy streets are easier to move out of the way and theaters are even easier, because land prices are high in busy cities and it is not easy to obtain so much space. The only way to remedy this is to specially build a central parking building to accommodate them. Currently, there are still few first-class large cities with this type of parking lot.

Regulations for Long-Distance Bus Travel

— Li Ji

Roads are the lifeline of a country, the foundation of transportation, and the tool of commerce. All countries in Europe and the United States attach importance to road construction. The cost in the annual financial budget is huge, and the construction plan is also the most perfect. Our country has recently learned from this and is actively carrying out road construction work, sparing no effort. The national roads that have been built already have more than 20,000 li, and the results are quite visible.

Now that each province in our country has provincial roads, and the interior is also opening up. The long-distance bus business is also developing at the same time, which makes the transportation between cities and towns extremely convenient. In this early stage of the rise of long-distance buses, although the local authorities encourage traffic, they should also pay attention to the driving regulations to avoid accidents and hinder construction.

In the United States, passengers who take public buses pay more than 1.5 trillion people a year. The caution and carelessness of drivers are related to people's livelihood and social peace. The National Long-Distance Bus Association of the United States has newly formulated a set of driving regulations for the safety of local people and passengers. It is quite valuable and can be used for reference and research by the automobile industry in our country. The full text is recorded below.

Service Notice

(1) Clean, comfortable, and safe machinery.

(2) Cautious, humble, and experienced drivers.

(3) Complete routes and accurate timing.

Service Key Points

(1) Safe Service

(A) Vehicles should be inspected frequently.

(B) Drivers must be physically and mentally healthy and have been trained and examined.

(C) Drivers must obey the rules and the instructions of traffic police, maintain order, and protect the highway.

(D) Regulate the driving time, distance, and speed to avoid accidents.

(2) Reliable Service

(A) Vehicles must be insured to prevent unexpected losses and to protect the interests of passengers.

(B) Sufficient capital and reduced expenses.

(C) Preserve lost items of passengers in order to claim them and devise ways to defend against pickpockets and petty thieves.

(3) Comfortable Service

(A) Ventilation, temperature, and light in the car must be suitable to increase the comfort of riding.

(B) The location and time of the transfer must be appropriate to make passengers feel convenient.

(C) Employees must be trained to treat passengers kindly and be thoughtful, and personally guide and instruct passengers anytime and anywhere.

Elephant Trunk Almighty

— Ji Ren

Rose is a famous elephant in the American circus. She is intelligent, docile, and agile. Her daily operations are no different from those of humans. She can even refuel and fill water. The illustration shows Rose opening the water tank cap of a Chevrolet six-cylinder car and pouring clear water. This kind of work is a daily routine, so her owner cherishes her very much.

Translations

Rare Automobile News from Around the World

— Lin

The success of car shock absorbers: German Captain Franz Karl Schleiff has recently invented a car shock absorber that can prevent passengers from being injured in car accidents. Mr. Schleiff recently tested this device three times in New York with great success. Initially, Mr. Schleiff drove a sports car at a speed of 26 miles per hour and crashed into the back of another sports car. The second time, the car was traveling at 18 miles per hour, and Mr. Schleiff drove the car towards a steel-concrete pillar and crashed into it. The third time, the car was traveling at nearly 30 miles per hour and crashed into a small car parked on the side of the road. The small car that was hit was destroyed. In these three tests, Mr. Schleiff was unharmed, but only suffered minor injuries during the last collision. During the test, Mr. Schleiff's crash absorber was installed on the sports car, and an electrical meter was used to record the car's speed at the time of the collision. This shock-absorbing crash device is shaped like an ordinary steel bumper bar. There is also a three-inch rubber plate that is parallel to the machine body and connected by steel scissors. When the car collides with the car, the rubber extends outward and the steel scissors also open, so the force of the collision is divided to the left and right, so that it is not related to the machine body. This device has special sales rights in Europe and the United States. The manufacturing location is in Germany.

General Motors' passenger car production: In 1929, the number of passenger cars registered in the United States was 22,599,701, of which 6,356,901 were produced by General Motors, that is, 28.13% of the registered number of various cars were produced by General Motors Corporation. This number is the same as the number of cars registered in the United States ten years ago. General Motors Manager Xuan Lesi said that this is a reward from customers for their satisfaction with General Motors cars.
